Here’s how it works: For Buyers: Buyers submit an offer for the domain name they’re interested in. The seller is then notified and can accept, decline, or counter the offer. DomainAgents ensures that buyers can negotiate without revealing their identity, helping to avoid price inflation based on who the buyer is. For Sellers: Sellers are notified of offers on their domains made by qualified buyers who have paid a fee upfront to engage the services of DomainAgents. This ensures that sellers only receive serious offers and can confidently evaluate buyer interest. Sellers can choose to accept, decline, or negotiate with the buyer, all while remaining in control of their domain. This system allows browsers to locate the server where the website is hosted.":"The Domain Name System, or DNS, is the unsung hero of internet navigation. This system allows browsers to locate the server where the website is hosted.","How DNS Resolution Works":"How DNS Resolution Works","Step 1: Query Initiation - When you enter a domain name, your computer sends a query to a DNS resolver, typically operated by your internet service provider.":"Step 1: Query Initiation - When you enter a domain name, your computer sends a query to a DNS resolver, typically operated by your internet service provider.","Step 2: Consulting the Name Servers - The resolver forwards the query to a series of DNS name servers, starting with the root server, then moving to the TLD server (like .com or .net), and finally to the authoritative name server for the specific domain.":"Step 2: Consulting the Name Servers - The resolver forwards the query to a series of DNS name servers, starting with the root server, then moving to the TLD server (like .com or .net), and finally to the authoritative name server for the specific domain.","Step 3: IP Address Retrieval - The authoritative name server returns the domain's corresponding IP address to the resolver.":"Step 3: IP Address Retrieval - The authoritative name server returns the domain's corresponding IP address to the resolver.","Step 4: Website Access - With the IP address obtained, your browser can then request the webpage from the web server, completing the connection.":"Step 4: Website Access - With the IP address obtained, your browser can then request the webpage from the web server, completing the connection.","Simplifying the Complexities":"Simplifying the Complexities","The Magic Behind the Scenes":"The Magic Behind the Scenes","This entire DNS process happens in milliseconds, a testament to the efficiency and sophistication of the system.
